=======
LEGEND
=======

Player = Cursor or CursorMove
@ = Cursor and Tile
Letter = LetterA or LetterB or LetterC or LetterD or LetterE or LetterF or LetterG or LetterH or LetterI or LetterJ or LetterK or LetterL or LetterM or LetterN or LetterO or LetterP or LetterQ or LetterR or LetterS or LetterT or LetterU or LetterV or LetterW or LetterX or LetterY or LetterZ
CursorSide = CursorHorz or CursorVert or CursorMoveHorz or CursorMoveVert
Edge = EdgeHorz or EdgeVert
Mk = Edge or Letter
- = EdgeHorz and Pno
| = EdgeVert and Pno

LetterBlue = A or E or O or T or L or R or N or S or LB1 or LB2
LetterGreen = P or H or M or D or I or LG1 or LG2
LetterYellow = G or B or C or W or U or LY1 or LY2
LetterRed = Y or K or F or 7
LetterPurple = J or Q or X or Z

GenericBlue = LetterBlue or PrizeBlue
GenericGreen = LetterGreen or PrizeGreen
GenericYellow = LetterYellow or PrizeYellow
GenericRed = LetterRed or PrizeRed
GenericPurple = LetterPurple or PrizePurple

Number = Number0 or Number1 or Number2 or Number3 or Number4 or Number5 or Number6 or Number7 or Number8 or Number9

Award = Award1 or Award2 or Award3 or Award4

COLLISIONLAYERS

Number, Award, LB1, LB2, LG1, LG2, LY1, LY2, LitSpawner

RULES
======

)
